## Section 021: Retry Backpressure Guidance
### Question 01: What decision does this reference help make?
- **current_section_observation:** Section 021 "Retry Backpressure Guidance", Question 01 on governing decision: the seed currently shows that the seed corpus-process bullets stand beside what the lineage implies for doctrine pressure, a rule contested in the living generation is relitigated there, not by retreating to the ancestor's fuller text as trump, ancestor content re-enters current practice only through recorded succession, a new revision citing what it restores, and repeated depth consultations on one topic signal the successor compressed too far there, feedback for its next revision rather than license to fork practice across generations
- **supporting_reason:** Section 021 "Retry Backpressure Guidance", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision matters because two live generations invite doctrine shopping, choosing whichever text supports a position, so lineage integrity depends on a single direction of authority for practice and a recorded channel for restoration
- **counterargument_or_limit:** Section 021 "Retry Backpressure Guidance", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision must not conceal this limit: the erosion path is silent forking, teams practicing from different generations without knowing it, each citing the family, until the shared vocabulary hides divergent rules
- **assumptions_and_boundaries:** Section 021 "Retry Backpressure Guidance", Question 01 on governing decision: apply the decision only within this boundary: dispute-handling across the generational boundary, within-generation dispute routing belongs to the successor's rubric-valve
